Andrew Boggeri< /name>
< review>
Tacos are really great. Reasonably priced and stuffed with meat. I'm usually a pretty big eater and found that three were enough for dinner. They have several meat options beyond just steak, chicken, carnitas. The al pastor was very good, maybe could be a little juicier and spicier. The carnitas was excellent, crispy and had some additional seasoning that I haven't encountered on carnitas before. They make their own horchata--it's not overly sweet or heavy like you often trying. Great place to sit outside and enjoy a beer in nice weather.</review>

You will always see work'n blokes chowing down on large plates of this delicious food to fuel them through the second half of their day.  I love going here when I'm positively hungry. <Name>J Dub< /Name>< Date>
1460707470275< /Date>
<Rating>5</Rating><Text>Best burrito place in Healdsburg, probably in Sonoma County! Almost everything they make is traditionally hand made from family recipes passed down from the old generation, but twisted just enough to fit "California Mexican" food while maintaining authenticity (but it's not a yuppie place at all).  Try the chicken fajita burrito. It's awesome! They also have some great veggie options, like the Burrito Guadalajara, which is not billed as vegan, but is simply delicious food that just HAPPENS to be vegan  (probably... I mean, at least it says on the menu it has no dairy or meat). I'm not a vegan, but I do appreciate scrumptious, healthy food...  and the Guadalajara burrito delivers!  The main thing that sets it apart is that this burrito has some nice veggies in it instead of just being a "regular burrito" with no meat (like most veggie burritos), so it's extra good!! Prices are still reasonable (especially for Healdsburg), staff is friendly, food comes out fast, place is clean, has a nice mural on one wall.  I highly recommend it, especially for burritos, but also for the rest of their food!< /Text><pictures>None< /pictures>< resp>
None< /resp>

<rate>1</rate>< review>
I recently scheduled an oil change/battery issues and replacement/remote start/smog test at Bobby's Pit stop.  All was going well until we received a phone call that the battery change would cost $195 (seemed a bit high) with supposedly a dead cell.  I called around to several other places and was quoted $100-125 with no service fee charged. I called in and requested not to do the battery change and mentioned much cheaper quotes elsewhere, guy on the phone talked to another and stated that it was due to a 30 minute service charge (30 minutes to replace a battery??).  When my wife went to pick up the car everyone was friendly, then when she went to turn the car on it wouldn't start. The dealership had turned the light to the on position (we always have it on Auto, no exceptions) and left it there, I'll let you draw your own conclusion as to whether or not it was intentional.  She acted nice, got a jump and left to Oil Can Henry's down the road.

There she was quickly and politely advised that her battery was testing fine at 80% Life approx, they  did a quick check and realized that the battery was low on water thus causing issues (apparently Bobby's doesn't check for this or prefers not to mention). The quickly filled it up and suggested waiting a couple days and said they didn't want to charge for work that wasn't necessary (ie replacing a perfectly good battery). My wife happily tipped $20 for the good service with multiple polite/profession service people at Oil Can Henry's and went on her way.

An hour later, battery works great, remote start running well and it was at no cost from a professional establishment.  Bobby's Pit stop overcharged, didn't do a thorough review of the battery and on top of all that I just realized today they didn't even provide or likely complete the smog test on our vehicle although they did charge for it.  Avoid this location at all costs and go to a reputable store right down the road.< /review>

< Review>
VERY disappointed

I usually have no interest in writing reviews after my experience at any location.
Unfortunately this time I feel I must share two of the most disappointing visits at this specific location.
I called in an order & asked for BR with NO CARROTS!
Surprisingly I received both of what I did not want.
Made perfect sense to me because as I was paying for my order I was watching the cook prepare the bowls and he continuously had to take chicken/steak off one bowl to put on to another and vice versa. Im not sure why any employee would be comfortable doing that in front of any customers... To add on on top of that neither the cook or the cashier covered the bowls as they were sliding out to close preparation.

<text>Great food. I'm not the biggest fan of ramen, but I like what they have to offer. Good broth, 5 different noodle options, and lots of tasty tidbits floating in the soup. Just had the katsu curry the other day and was hugely impressed. Came out super hot, good sized serving of crispy chicken, and LOTS of sauce and rice to accompany.

< review>
Small restaurant and can often be crowded.  Haven't had issues finding a parking spot but sometimes a short wait especially during lunch.  The ingredients are fresh for example they use real corn kernels and not frozen which I appreciate.  The noodles are perfectly cooked and not mushy (al dente).  The broth is light and not salty unless of course you choose the salt base.  Overall the ramen is excellent.

My only small complaint is that there is no substituting even if the ingredient is the same price if bought separately as an add on.  I didn't want to spend the price of the create your own bowl and only wanted to replace the bamboo shoots of one of the smaller bowls with corn.  I would have had to paid for the corn separately.  I kind of understand though.</review>

<user>108669571891821746281</user><review>Gomen is my go-to ramen spot near Cypress! Always order the kakuni deluxe with spinach (or sometimes kale) noodles and on healthier nights I'll go with chicken over the pork. Be warned, the chicken comes out more dry than the chashu (pork). I've had really delicious ramen broth in little Tokyo and in Japan, and this place is probably the closest tasting in our area. The service is quick and if you come before 6pm you'll beat the crowd. Their gyoza used to be better, but the last few times I've gotten it was meh (probably because it was packed and they were just rushing to get food out to the customers) instead of being lightly crispy it was mushy. Their takoyaki is good, wish the piece of octopus inside was bigger though. Will definitely be back here for my fix in another month.</review>< gmapID>

<UserId.>104894477574690414472</UserId.><Name>Felix Pham<//Name><date>1499394051786</date>< Rating>
4< /Rating>
<text>Service (one of two stars)
Accommodates water, dishware, and silverware at an appropriate pace. When ordering a custom order they will give you a paper to fill out. Unfortunately they speak very little English, but I would say this adds to the authentic experience.

Food quality (1.5 of two stars)
The ordered food was edible and consistent with what I expect a Ramen to taste like. The bowls and plates were themes but look like they came from Daiso. They have cold noodles for the summertime and Japanese people can be seen dining here - which means they must be doing something right.

Ambiance (one of one star)
It is clear they are a Ramen restaurant that has been modified to meet the American culture. They reasonably price their food.
Nice lighting, plain paintings, a manga library, a few gundamn figures, and T-shirt uniforms to identify employees. The employees greet you in Japanese, which give the experience authenticity. Parking is abundant.

Overall a nice family owned restaurant with some hired help. 3.5 stars, I'll round up 4. I will be back to curb my Ramen cravings from time to time.</text><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< response>

< Review>
Sweet modern little Ramen place with wide range of broth and flavor options, excellent fast service, and nice spacious interior.
We ate both soy sauce and miso ramen noodles and they were flavorful and clean tasting, not greasy. Our order also came surprisingly fast.
Gyoza dumplings were crispy with vegetable filling.
Mochi ice cream and almond jelly were excellent.
Check their hours before planning a visit, they are closed after lunch like so many Japanese restaurants.
Definitely worth a trip.<//Review>

<userid>102918253898437847981< /userid><rate>4<//rate><GmapID>0x80dd292f377d7309:0xc2f4ae4462ecf97< /GmapID><text>Go forth, Go prosper, Gomen

LALALA Ramen pass stop #1

50% off spicy tonkotsu miso ramen

Deciding to lunch at Gomen during the designated LALALA Ramen pass hours, apparently I wasn't the only one.  The place was packed with diners with the same idea.  However, the wait time was only around 10 minutes, so it wasn't long before my slurpfest commenced.

Sitting at the counter, I couldn't wait to dive into my bowl of spicy tonkotsu miso ramen.

Of course, I had to add white & red pepper, along with chili oil to kick things up a notch to my liking.

The spicy tonkotsu miso ramen did not disappoint!  Delicious broth, al dente noodles, a few slivers of pork and the rest of the gang warmed my tummy.  Some people like to sweat out toxins in the sauna.  I, however, like to sweat out toxins by eating spicy foods!  The floodgates of my sweat glands opened up as I tore into each fiery spoonful of broth.  My fellow ramen lovers with me at the counter were also sweating it out to the oldies with me ;p  I would've preferred the egg to be runny, as opposed to hardboiled, but knowing that some ramen places charge extra for egg, it's only a minor gripe.  Also, the amount of pork, while tasting good, seemed to be lacking.  Of course, seeing how my bowl of ramen only cost $4.25 + tax, maybe that's the reason why for the apparently miniscule amount of meat.

I was as happy as a fly on dog poop, savoring each slurp & gulp of my piping hot bowl of ramen until I proudly registered myself as an upstanding member of the Clean Plate Club.

Service was sufficient, as tables were promptly cleaned & readied for waiting guests.  Seating for 5 at the counter, with tables packed with ramen lovers throughout the rest of the restaurant.  Parking is in a private lot & can be hard to come by, depending upon when you go.

Gomen, domo arigato!  Your spicy tonkotsu miso ramen hit the spot just right!  My first stop with my LALALA Ramen Pass was a winner!  When I come back, and oh yes, I will be back, I'll have to order your highly regarded kakuni ramen.  Until then, sayonara!

Highly recommend!
